## 评论 (1 条)

### 评论 #1 — ROCmSupport (2021-04-05T11:46:10Z)

Thanks @FireCulex for reaching out.
This issue is no more observed with ROCm 4.1, which is the latest version. I recommend to try with the same.
And also always recommend to try with the official supported OS versions like Ubuntu 18.04.5 or 20.04.2 etc.,.
Feel free to open a new issue, if any, for quick resolution.
Thank you.
